<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Case_statistics">Case statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Case statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic#Case_statistics" title="Timeline of the COVID-19 pandemic">Timeline of the COVID-19 pandemic §&nbsp;Case statistics</a></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Pandemic_chronology">Pandemic chronology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pandemic chronology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1_February">1 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 1 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Log-linear_plot_of_coronavirus_cases_with_linear_regressions.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Log-linear_plot_of_coronavirus_cases_with_linear_regressions.png/220px-Log-linear_plot_of_coronavirus_cases_with_linear_regressions.png" decoding="async" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Log-linear_plot_of_coronavirus_cases_with_linear_regressions.png/330px-Log-linear_plot_of_coronavirus_cases_with_linear_regressions.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Log-linear_plot_of_coronavirus_cases_with_linear_regressions.png/440px-Log-linear_plot_of_coronavirus_cases_with_linear_regressions.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="700" width="220" height="193"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Log-linear_plot_of_coronavirus_cases_with_linear_regressions.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Semi-log_plot" title="Semi-log plot">Semi-log plot</a> of <a href="/wiki/Cumulative_incidence" title="Cumulative incidence">cumulative incidence</a> of confirmed cases and deaths in China and the rest of the world<sup id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BNO_News_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BNO_News-3">[3]</a></sup></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:NCoV20200209_Hubei_China_ROW_cases.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/NCoV20200209_Hubei_China_ROW_cases.png/220px-NCoV20200209_Hubei_China_ROW_cases.png" decoding="async" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/NCoV20200209_Hubei_China_ROW_cases.png/330px-NCoV20200209_Hubei_China_ROW_cases.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/NCoV20200209_Hubei_China_ROW_cases.png/440px-NCoV20200209_Hubei_China_ROW_cases.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="700" width="220" height="193"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:NCoV20200209_Hubei_China_ROW_cases.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Semi-log_plot" title="Semi-log plot">Semi-log plot</a> of daily <a href="/wiki/Incidence_(epidemiology)" title="Incidence (epidemiology)">incidence (epidemiology)</a> of cases by region: Hubei Province; mainland China excluding Hubei; the rest of the world (ROW); and the world total.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-4">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:NCoV20200223_daily_deaths_by_region.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/NCoV20200223_daily_deaths_by_region.png/220px-NCoV20200223_daily_deaths_by_region.png" decoding="async" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/NCoV20200223_daily_deaths_by_region.png/330px-NCoV20200223_daily_deaths_by_region.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/NCoV20200223_daily_deaths_by_region.png/440px-NCoV20200223_daily_deaths_by_region.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="700" width="220" height="193"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:NCoV20200223_daily_deaths_by_region.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Semi-log plot of coronavirus daily deaths by region: Hubei Province; mainland China excluding Hubei; the rest of the world (ROW); and the world total<sup id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BNO_News_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BNO_News-3">[3]</a></sup></div></div></div>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 12:<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> (Please note that the WHO Situation Reports as official reportage stand on their own.)
</p>
<ul><li>Australia reported another three cases, including the first two cases in <a href="/wiki/South_Australia" title="South Australia">South Australia</a>, bringing their total to 12.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan reported three more cases, increasing their total to 20.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirms two more cases, bringing the total to 18.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed the twelfth case of the coronavirus: a 49-year-old Chinese man who works as a Japanese tour guide in western <a href="/wiki/Seoul,_South_Korea" class="mw-redirect" title="Seoul, South Korea">Seoul</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
<li>Spain confirmed its first case of the virus on La Gomera in the Canaries.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United States of America reported its eighth case, a man from <a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">Boston</a> who recently returned to college after traveling to Wuhan.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></li>
<li>Vietnam confirmed its sixth case in <a href="/wiki/Kh%C3%A1nh_H%C3%B2a_Province" title="Khánh Hòa Province">Khánh Hòa Province</a>, another domestic transmission in direct contact.<sup id="cite_ref-VN_declare_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VN_declare-13">[13]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2_February">2 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 2 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 13:<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>India announced its second case.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li>Philippines, saw the first confirmed death from COVID-19 outside mainland China announced. The case was that of a 44-year-old male who was the companion of the first confirmed case in the country; both are Chinese nationals from Wuhan who had arrived in the country via Hong Kong on 21 January. He had been in stable condition prior to his death on 1 February.<sup id="cite_ref-phdied_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-phdied-16">[16]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea reported three more cases, bringing their total to 15.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup></li>
<li>United Arab Emirates reported its fifth case.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United States of America, confirmed three more cases, all in California, bringing the total to 11.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup> Two Germans aboard the evacuation flight from Wuhan tested positive for the virus, bringing the number of cases there up to twelve.<sup id="cite_ref-DW_2020-02-03_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DW_2020-02-03-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li>Vietnam announced its seventh case of COVID-19, a Vietnamese-American who had had a two-hour layover at Wuhan Airport.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="3_February">3 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 3 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 14:<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup>
</p><p>The number of deaths in Hubei outside Wuhan reached 101.
</p><p>According to WHO, there were no new countries reporting cases in the past 24 hours.
</p>
<ul><li>India confirmed its third case in <a href="/wiki/Kerala" title="Kerala">Kerala</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup></li>
<li>Vietnam announced its eighth COVID-19 case, a Vietnamese woman who had been on the same flight with three other positive cases.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="4_February">4 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 4 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 15:<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Belgium confirmed its first case, bringing the total in the European Union to 24.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed its first death from a 39-year-old patient, the thirteenth confirmed case in the city.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia confirmed two more COVID-19 cases, which included a Malaysian citizen, bringing the total to 10 cases.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed six more cases, including the first locally transmitted cases involving four, bringing the total to 24. Two others came from an evacuation plane from Wuhan.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed its 16th case after a tourist returned from Thailand, the first to have been infected there.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li>Thailand confirmed six more cases, bringing the total to 25.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup></li>
<li>Vietnam announced its ninth and tenth COVID-19 case, including a Vietnamese man who had been on the same flight with four other positive cases.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="5_February">5 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 5 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 16:<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>China, in Wuhan now reported 10,117 cases in total, exceeding 10,000.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup>  Tianjin, reported its first death.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup>   Chinese experts said that nucleic acid testing was only able to identify 30%-50% positive cases.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed three more cases, bringing the total to 21.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed 10 new cases from the quarantined cruise ship <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, near Yokohama, bringing the total number up to 35 cases. There were more than 3,500 on board to be tested.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia announced two more cases, bringing the total cases to 12.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup></li>
<li>Philippines confirmed its third positive case, a 60-year-old woman from Wuhan, China.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed four more cases, including a six-month-old Singaporean, bringing the total cases to 28.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed two more cases of COVID-19, including a patient who returned from Singapore, bringing the total cases to 18.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup> Another case was later reported, bringing the total cases to 19.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United States of America, saw Health officials in the state of Wisconsin announce the first case in that state.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[46]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="6_February">6 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 6 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 17:<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Canada announced 2 presumptive cases in <a href="/wiki/British_Columbia" title="British Columbia">British Columbia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup></li>
<li>China, In Zhejiang over 1,000 cases were confirmed, the first such province besides Hubei.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup>  Doctor <a href="/wiki/Li_Wenliang" title="Li Wenliang">Li Wenliang</a>, who notified his class colleagues in a private chat room  on social media of the coronavirus, died of the infection.<sup id="cite_ref-auto23_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto23-50">[50]</a></sup></li>
<li>Germany confirmed its thirteenth case, and Italy confirmed its third, bringing the total number of confirmed cases in Europe to 31.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed three more cases, bringing the total to 24.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed another 10 new cases from <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, quarantined in Yokohama, bringing the total to 45.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia confirmed two more cases, bringing the total to 14. One of the cases was locally transmitted, the first in Malaysia.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed two more cases, bringing the total to 30.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">[56]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed four more cases, bringing the total to 23.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan announced three more cases, bringing the total to 16.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United Kingdom saw the third case confirmed, with the patient having visited Singapore.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup></li>
<li>A patient in San Jose, California became the first Covid-19 death in the United States discovered by April 2020. She died at home without any known recent foreign travel, after being unusually sick from flu in late January, then recovering, working from home, and suddenly dying on February 6. A February 7 autopsy<sup id="cite_ref-dowdautopsy_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dowdautopsy-60">[60]</a></sup> was completed in April (after virus tests on tissue samples) and attributed the death to Transmural Myocardial Ischemia (Infarction) with a Minor Component of Myocarditis due to COVID-19 Infection.  Her case indicates that community transmission was happening undetected in the US, most likely since December.<sup id="cite_ref-sfchron22apr_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sfchron22apr-61">[61]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:1_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-62">[62]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-latimes21apr_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-latimes21apr-63">[63]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-latimes22apr_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-latimes22apr-64">[64]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup></li>
<li>Vietnam confirmed two more cases, bringing the total to 12.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="7_February">7 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 7 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 18:<sup id="cite_ref-WHOsituationreport_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WHOsituationreport-67">[67]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>China
<ul><li>Guangdong confirmed over 1,000 cases in total, the second such province outside Hubei, and recorded its first death.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup></li>
<li>Wuhan reported 67 more deaths, bringing the total number of people killed by the virus there to 545; other cities in Hubei reported 14 deaths in total, their net figure now reaching 154.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gansu" title="Gansu">Gansu</a> recorded its first death.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li></ul></li>
<li>Another 41 tested positive for the coronavirus on <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, bringing the total number of cases in Japan to 86.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">[70]</a></sup></li>
<li>Germany announced its fourteenth case.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">[71]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed 2 more cases, bringing the total number to 26.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">[72]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia confirmed one more case from a tourist entering from Singapore, bringing the total to 15.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">[73]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">[74]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed three more cases, bringing the total to 33. Most of these cases were initially of unknown origin, causing the Disease Outbreak Response System Condition (DORSCON) level to increase to Orange.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">[75]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DORSCON_Orange_76-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DORSCON_Orange-76">[76]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed one more case, bringing the total to 24.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup></li>
<li>Vietnam confirmed one additional case, bringing the total to 13.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">[79]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="8_February">8 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 8 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 19:<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">[80]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>China:
<ul><li>Wuhan confirmed 63 more deaths, bringing its total to 608;<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup> this now includes a Japanese citizen and a US citizen dying on this day.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup></li>
<li>Henan became the third province besides Hubei to report over 1,000 cases.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup> Nationally, the number of cases outside Hubei exceeded 10,000.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-85">[85]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Aerosol" title="Aerosol">Aerosol</a> was confirmed as a medium of transmission for the first time.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup></li>
<li>Beijing reported a first type of case involving a patient, who tested positive after three negative test results, and <a href="/wiki/Qingtian_County" title="Qingtian County">Qingtian</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zhejiang" title="Zhejiang">Zhejiang</a> reported a case where the patient tested positive only after being tested for the fifth time.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>France confirmed five cases involving British nationals, bringing the total number to 11.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan, three more cases tested positive on <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, bringing the total number of cases in Japan to 89.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia confirmed one more case, bringing the total to 16.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed seven more cases, bringing the total to 40.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup></li>
<li>Thailand confirmed seven additional cases, bringing the total to 32.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">[93]</a></sup></li>
<li>United Arab Emirates confirmed two more cases, bringing the total to seven.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">[94]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="9_February">9 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 9 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 20:<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>China (Mainland) now confirmed a total of 40,213 cases, exceeding 40,000, of which 29,631 were in Hubei.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">[96]</a></sup>  The coronavirus death toll in China rose to 811, surpassing the toll from the <a href="/wiki/SARS" class="mw-redirect" title="SARS">SARS</a> epidemic from 2002–03.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">[97]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed ten more cases, with nine from the same family, bringing the total number to 36.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">[98]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 17.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">[99]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number to 43.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">[100]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">[101]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea reported three new cases of the virus, bringing the country's total to 27.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">[102]</a></sup></li>
<li>Spain confirmed the second case in the country in <a href="/wiki/Palma_de_Mallorca" title="Palma de Mallorca">Palma de Mallorca</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[103]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed its eighteenth case.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">[104]</a></sup></li>
<li>United Kingdom confirmed its fourth case.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">[105]</a></sup></li>
<li>Vietnam confirmed its fourteenth case, a 55-year-old woman in <a href="/wiki/V%C4%A9nh_Ph%C3%BAc" class="mw-redirect" title="Vĩnh Phúc">Vĩnh Phúc</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">[106]</a></sup></li>
<li>Six more cases were confirmed aboard <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, bringing the total number of cases on the ship to 70, with Japan having 96 cases.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">[107]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">[108]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="10_February">10 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 10 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 21:<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">[109]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Hong Kong confirmed six more cases, bringing the total number to 42.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">[110]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed 65 more cases on <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, bringing the total to 135.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia confirmed one more case involving a citizen, bringing the total to 18.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">[113]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed another two cases including a <a href="/wiki/Certis_Group" title="Certis Group">Certis</a> officer who served Quarantine Orders, bringing the total to 45.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup></li>
<li>United Arab Emirates confirmed its eighth case, an Indian national.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">[115]</a></sup></li>
<li>United Kingdom saw four additional cases were confirmed, bringing the total to eight. The transmission in these cases is believed to have occurred in France.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">[116]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">[117]</a></sup></li>
<li>United States of America confirmed its thirteenth case in <a href="/wiki/San_Diego" title="San Diego">San Diego</a>, a patient who had been evacuated from Wuhan.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">[118]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="11_February">11 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 11 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 22:<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">[119]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Germany confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 16.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">[120]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed seven more cases, bringing the total to 49.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">[121]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed another two cases, bringing the total to 47.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">[122]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed one more case, a 30-year-old Chinese woman, bringing the total number to 28.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">[123]</a></sup></li>
<li>Thailand confirmed one new cases, bringing the total in the country to 33.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">[124]</a></sup></li>
<li>Vietnam confirmed its fifteenth case, a three-month-old baby infected by her grandmother.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">[125]</a></sup></li>
<li>WHO gives the disease the new name <a href="/wiki/COVID-19" class="mw-redirect" title="COVID-19">COVID-19</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">[126]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">[127]</a></sup> Additionally, the virus itself is named <a href="/wiki/Severe_acute_respiratory_syndrome_coronavirus_2" title="Severe acute respiratory syndrome coronavirus 2">SARS-CoV-2</a>.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="12_February">12 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 12 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 23:<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Hong Kong confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 50.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">[129]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">[130]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed 39 more cases on <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, including one quarantine officer, bringing the total to 174.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup> Another case was reported in Japan itself, bringing the total number to 29.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">[132]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed three more cases, bringing the total to 50.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">[134]</a></sup> Earlier, 300 employees of <a href="/wiki/DBS_Bank" title="DBS Bank">DBS Bank</a> were asked to evacuate from the office at <a href="/wiki/Marina_Bay_Financial_Centre" title="Marina Bay Financial Centre">Marina Bay Financial Centre</a> Tower 3 due to a confirmed case there.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">[135]</a></sup></li>
<li>United Kingdom - The first case in London was confirmed, bringing the country's total to 9.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">[136]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup></li>
<li>United States of America confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 14.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">[138]</a></sup></li>
<li>First Commercially Released Song is released about the Coronavirus - <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IBDIYGtDGJQ">Coronavirus Patient Zero</a> - by Australian Singer-Songwriter <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://jasonpenna.com/">Jason Penna</a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="13_February">13 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 13 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 24:<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">[139]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Japan confirmed four more cases, bringing the total to 33.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">[140]</a></sup> At the same time, 44 new cases were confirmed on the <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, bringing the total to 218.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">[141]</a></sup> Later on, Japan confirmed its first death from the virus.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">[142]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">[143]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number to 53.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">[144]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 19.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">[145]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed eight more cases, bringing the total number to 58. A school in <a href="/wiki/National_University_of_Singapore" title="National University of Singapore">National University of Singapore</a> will conduct e-learning from 14 to 21 February as a precaution after one of the cases involved a professor.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">[146]</a></sup></li>
<li>Unites States of America, the CDC confirmed the 15th US coronavirus case, a Wuhan evacuee quarantined at a military base in <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">[147]</a></sup></li>
<li>Vietnam confirmed its 16th case.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Discrepancy_in_the_number_of_cases">Discrepancy in the number of cases</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Discrepancy in the number of cases">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The same day, Hubei reported newly confirmed cases of 14,840, nearly 10 times more than the previous day, while deaths more than doubled to 242. This was due to the change in definition that included clinical (radiological) diagnosis of patients.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup> The World Health Organization indicated that for consistency it would report only the number of laboratory-confirmed  cases.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="14_February">14 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 14 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 25:<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Canada confirmed <a href="/wiki/British_Columbia" title="British Columbia">British Columbia</a>'s fifth presumptive case, bringing the total number in the country to 8.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup></li>
<li>Egypt confirmed its first case, a foreigner of undisclosed nationality. This was the first case on the African continent.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed three more infections, bringing the total number to 56.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed four more cases, bringing the total number to 37.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed nine more cases, bringing the total number to 67.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">[158]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="15_February">15 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: 15 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 26:<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>France saw the first death outside Asia being confirmed, an 80 year old Chinese tourist in France. The country also confirmed its 12th case.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">[161]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed nine additional confirmed cases not aboard <i>Diamond Princess</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup> Japan also confirmed 67 additional cases aboard the cruise ship <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, bringing the total number of cases from the ship to 285.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">[163]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">[164]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia confirmed three more cases, including an American passenger from the cruise ship <a href="/wiki/MS_Westerdam" title="MS Westerdam">MS&nbsp;<i>Westerdam</i></a> flying from Cambodia, bringing the total number to 22.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">[165]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:0_166-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-166">[166]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">[167]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed five more cases, bringing the total number to 72.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup></li>
<li>Thailand confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 34.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="16_February">16 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 16 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 27:<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">[170]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Hong Kong confirmed one new coronavirus case, bringing the total to 57.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">[171]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan also confirmed six new cases, bringing the total of infected people not aboard <i>Diamond Princess</i> to 59.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">[172]</a></sup> 70 additional cases were confirmed on <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, increasing the tally to 355.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">[173]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number to 75.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">[174]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 29.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">[175]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed its first death from COVID-19, a man in his 60s. Moreover, two new cases were confirmed, bringing the total number to 20.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">[176]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">[177]</a></sup></li>
<li>United Arab Emirates confirmed one more case, a 37-year-old Chinese citizen, bringing the total number to 9.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">[178]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="17_February">17 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 17 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 28:<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">[179]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Hong Kong confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number to 60.<sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">[180]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed seven new cases, bringing the total of infected people not aboard <i>Diamond Princess</i> to 66. <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a> in Japan confirmed 99 new coronavirus cases, bringing the total number of infected people on the cruise ship to 454.<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">[181]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 77.<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">[182]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 30.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">[183]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 22.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">[184]</a></sup></li>
<li>Thailand confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 35.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">[185]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United States had its second known death from Covid-19, from unknown (community) transmission to a 69-year-old man in Santa Clara County, California.  This death was attributed to Covid-19 in April by a delayed autopsy.<sup id="cite_ref-sfchron22apr_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sfchron22apr-61">[61]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-latimes22apr_64-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-latimes22apr-64">[64]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="18_February">18 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 18 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 29:<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">[186]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Hong Kong confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 62.<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">[187]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed eight more cases across the nation, bringing the total to 74. At the same time, 88 additional cases aboard <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a> were confirmed, bringing the total on the ship to 542.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">[188]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed four more cases, bringing the total number to 81.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">[189]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 31.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">[190]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="19_February">19 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: 19 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 30:<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">[191]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Hong Kong confirmed its second death from the coronavirus. In addition, three new cases were confirmed, bringing the total number in Hong Kong to 65.<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">[192]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iran confirmed its first two cases resulting in deaths.<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">[193]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number to 84.<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">[194]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed 20 more cases, bringing the total number to 51 with the majority of these transmissions happening in a church in Daegu.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">[195]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 23.<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">[196]</a></sup></li>
<li>Passengers started to disembark from <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, one of the cruise ships in the outbreak. The sheer number of passengers infected has led to questions over the effectiveness of quarantine measures.<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">[197]</a></sup> 79 more cases are confirmed on the cruise ship, bringing the total number to 621.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">[198]</a></sup> Japan also reported 10 new cases not aboard the cruise ship.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="20_February">20 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: 20 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 31:<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">[199]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Hong Kong confirmed four more cases, bringing the total number to 69.<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">[200]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iran confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number to five.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">[201]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed ten more domestic cases, bringing the total number to 94.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">[202]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 85.<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">[203]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed 53 more cases, bringing the total number to 104. The first death from the virus was also confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-DP20Feb_204-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DP20Feb-204">[204]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">[205]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 24.<sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">[206]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United States confirmed one more case in California, bringing the total number to 16.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">[207]</a></sup></li>
<li>Two deaths were confirmed aboard the cruise ship <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a> along with 13 more cases, bringing the total number to 634.<sup id="cite_ref-DP20Feb_204-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DP20Feb-204">[204]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="21_February">21 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: 21 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 32:<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">[208]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Australia confirmed four more cases involving evacuees from the cruise ship <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, bringing the total number to 19.<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">[209]</a></sup></li>
<li>Canada confirms one more case, a woman who had recently visited Iran, bringing the total number to nine.<sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">[210]</a></sup></li>
<li>Israel also confirmed its first case, an evacuee from <i>Diamond Princess</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">[211]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-telegraph.co.uk_212-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraph.co.uk-212">[212]</a></sup></li>
<li>Italy confirmed 17 cases, bringing the total number to 20. Authorities also reported the first death, a 78-year-old man.<sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">[213]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">[214]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">[215]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">[216]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">[217]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iran announces 13 new cases, bringing the total to 18. Two more deaths were also confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraph.co.uk_212-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraph.co.uk-212">[212]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed 15 more cases, bringing the total number to 109.<sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">[218]</a></sup></li>
<li>Lebanon confirmed its first case.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraph.co.uk_212-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraph.co.uk-212">[212]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 86.<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">[219]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed 100 more cases, bringing the total number to 204.<sup id="cite_ref-SKorea21Feb_220-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SKorea21Feb-220">[220]</a></sup> The country also reported its second death.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">[221]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 26.<sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">[222]</a></sup></li>
<li>United Arab Emirates confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 11.<sup id="cite_ref-223" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-223">[223]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United States confirmed 20 more cases, bringing the total number to 35.<sup id="cite_ref-224" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-224">[224]</a></sup> Furthermore, the <a href="/wiki/Association_of_Public_Health_Laboratories" title="Association of Public Health Laboratories">Association of Public Health Laboratories</a> (APHL) announced that only three states were capable of testing for the corona virus: California, Nebraska, and Illinois.<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">[225]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="22_February">22 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: 22 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 33:<sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">[226]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Australia confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number to 22.<sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">[227]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 70.<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">[228]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iran confirmed 10 more cases, bringing the total number to 28. A fifth death was also confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">[229]</a></sup></li>
<li>Italy confirmed 59 more cases spread across three different administrative regions, bringing the total number to 79, making Italy the European country with the biggest number of cases of coronavirus infections.<sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">[230]</a></sup> The second death was also confirmed, an Italian woman from Lombardy.<sup id="cite_ref-231" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-231">[231]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed 26 more cases, bringing the total number to 135.<sup id="cite_ref-232" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-232">[232]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number to 89.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233">[233]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed 229 more cases, bringing the total number to 433.<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">[234]</a></sup> Concerns are raised that 9 tourists from South Korea may have caused a widespread exposure in Israel.<sup id="cite_ref-235" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-235">[235]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United Arab Emirates confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 13.<sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">[236]</a></sup></li>
<li>The urine sample of a patient tested positive.<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">[237]</a></sup></li>
<li>A genome analysis indicated that the virus in <a href="/wiki/Huanan_Seafood_Market" class="mw-redirect" title="Huanan Seafood Market">Huanan Seafood Market</a> originated from outside.<sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238">[238]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="23_February">23 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: 23 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 34:<sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">[239]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Canada confirmed one more presumptive case in Ontario. The samples had been sent to the National Microbiology Lab for further testing.<sup id="cite_ref-240" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-240">[240]</a></sup> Later, the cases was confirmed positive, bringing the total number to 10.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed four more cases, bringing the total number to 74.<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">[241]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iran confirmed 15 more cases and two more deaths, bringing the total number to 43 and 8 respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-242" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-242">[242]</a></sup></li>
<li>Israel confirmed one more case, who was a passenger on the cruise ship, bringing the total number to 2.<sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243">[243]</a></sup></li>
<li>Italy confirmed 73 new cases, bringing the total to 152 spread across five different administrative regions.<sup id="cite_ref-ansa.it_244-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ansa.it-244">[244]</a></sup> The third death was also reported.<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">[245]</a></sup> Italy is now the third country in the world by number of cases, after China and South Korea.<sup id="cite_ref-ansa.it_244-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ansa.it-244">[244]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed 169 more cases, bringing the total number to 602. Four more deaths were also confirmed, bringing the total to 6.<sup id="cite_ref-246" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-246">[246]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCSKorea23Feb_247-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCSKorea23Feb-247">[247]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 28.<sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248">[248]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United Kingdom confirmed four new cases, all involving evacuees from the Diamond Princess cruise ship, bringing the total number to 13.<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249">[249]</a></sup></li>
<li>There were 57 more cases aboard <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, bringing the total number to 691. One death associated to the cruise ship was also confirmed, bringing the total number to 3.<sup id="cite_ref-250" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-250">[250]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="24_February">24 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: 24 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 35:<sup id="cite_ref-251" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-251">[251]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Afghanistan confirmed its first case involving a person who recently returned from the Iranian city of Qom.<sup id="cite_ref-252" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-252">[252]</a></sup></li>
<li>Bahrain confirmed its first case involving a Bahraini citizen who travelled to Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-253" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-253">[253]</a></sup></li>
<li>Canada confirmed one more case in British Columbia, bringing the total number to 11.<sup id="cite_ref-254" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254">[254]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed seven more cases, bringing the total number to 81.<sup id="cite_ref-255" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-255">[255]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iran confirmed 18 more cases, bringing the total number to 61. Four more deaths were also reported in the country, bringing the total number to 12.<sup id="cite_ref-256" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-256">[256]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iraq confirmed its first case involving an Iranian student.<sup id="cite_ref-AA24Feb_257-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AA24Feb-257">[257]</a></sup></li>
<li>Italy confirmed 74 new cases, bringing the total to 229 spread across six different administrative regions.<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258">[258]</a></sup> Four more deaths were also confirmed, bringing the total number to 7.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259">[259]</a></sup></li>
<li>Kuwait announced their first cases involving five people arriving from the Iranian city of Mashhad.<sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260">[260]</a></sup></li>
<li>Oman confirmed its first cases involving two Omani women who had come from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261">[261]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-STOman24Feb_262-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-STOman24Feb-262">[262]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 90.<sup id="cite_ref-263" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-263">[263]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed 231 more cases, bringing the total number to 833. The seventh death was also confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-264" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-264">[264]</a></sup></li>
<li>Spain confirmed its third positive case, an Italian man, in Tenerife, Canary Islands.<sup id="cite_ref-265" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-265">[265]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 30.<sup id="cite_ref-266" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-266">[266]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United States confirmed 18 more cases including evacuated passengers from the cruise ship, bringing the total number to 53.<sup id="cite_ref-267" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-267">[267]</a></sup></li>
<li>A patient in <a href="/wiki/Sichuan" title="Sichuan">Sichuan</a> province tested positive only on her 9th test.<sup id="cite_ref-268" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-268">[268]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="25_February">25 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: 25 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 36:<sup id="cite_ref-269" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-269">[269]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Algeria reported its first case, an Italian man who arrived on 17 February.<sup id="cite_ref-270" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-270">[270]</a></sup></li>
<li>Austria reported its first two cases, two Italians living in Tyrol tested positive for the coronavirus.<sup id="cite_ref-271" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-271">[271]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272">[272]</a></sup> One of the couple was a receptionist at a hotel and as a result the hotel in the Alpine tourist hub of Innsbruck was sealed off in an effort to contain the outbreak.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li>Bahrain confirmed its second case, a Bahraini woman who had travelled from Iran through Dubai International Airport.<sup id="cite_ref-273" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-273">[273]</a></sup> This later increased to eight confirmed cases with the addition of two Bahraini men and four Saudi Arabian women.<sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274">[274]</a></sup> Later on the same day, Bahrain updated the number of cases to 17, with all infected people travelling from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-275" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-275">[275]</a></sup>  This total later rose again to 23 cases, again all having travelled from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-276" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-276">[276]</a></sup></li>
<li>Brazil Ministry of Health reported the first positive case of coronavirus in the country and South America, a 61-year-old man from <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="São Paulo">São Paulo</a>, who travelled to <a href="/wiki/Lombardy" title="Lombardy">Lombardy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>, between 9 and 21 February. He was showing mild symptoms and quarantined at home, the confirmation test was also positive.<sup id="cite_ref-277" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-277">[277]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-278" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-278">[278]</a></sup></li>
<li>Croatia announced its first case of the virus, with a patient hospitalised in the capital, Zagreb, who had travelled to Italy and stayed in Milan.<sup id="cite_ref-279" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-279">[279]</a></sup></li>
<li>France saw two additional cases: one was a French man returning from a trip in the Lombardy region of Italy; the other was a young Chinese woman returning to France from a trip to China. This took the total number of cases in the country to 14.<sup id="cite_ref-280" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-280">[280]</a></sup></li>
<li>Germany saw a case identified in the state of North Rhine-Westphalia of a person recently returned from Italy, taking the country's cases to 17. Another man was later confirmed to be positive, bringing the total number to 18.<sup id="cite_ref-281" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-281">[281]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number to 84.<sup id="cite_ref-282" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-282">[282]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iranian officials confirmed the death toll was officially now 16. There were 34 more cases, bringing the total number to 95.<sup id="cite_ref-283" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-283">[283]</a></sup> The same day, Iranian MP <a href="/wiki/Mahmoud_Sadeghi" title="Mahmoud Sadeghi">Mahmoud Sadeghi</a> confirmed he had tested positive for the virus,<sup id="cite_ref-284" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-284">[284]</a></sup> along with <a href="/wiki/Iraj_Harirchi" title="Iraj Harirchi">Iraj Harirchi</a>, the Deputy Minister for Health, who had the previous day been part of a press conference about Iran's handling of the virus.<sup id="cite_ref-285" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-285">[285]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iraq confirmed five more cases - an Iranian student and a family of four who had arrived from Iran, taking the total number of cases to 6.<sup id="cite_ref-286" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-286">[286]</a></sup></li>
<li>Italy confirmed 94 new cases, bringing the total to 323 spread across nine different administrative regions. Three more deaths were also confirmed, bringing the total number to 10.<sup id="cite_ref-287" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-287">[287]</a></sup> This later in the day rose to four deaths, bringing the total to 11.<sup id="cite_ref-288" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-288">[288]</a></sup></li>
<li>Kuwait confirmed four additional cases, all of them people who had returned from Iran, taking their total to 9 cases.<sup id="cite_ref-289" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-289">[289]</a></sup></li>
<li>Oman confirmed two additional cases, taking its total to four cases.  Both the additional cases were linked to travel to Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-290" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-290">[290]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 91.<sup id="cite_ref-291" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-291">[291]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed 144 more cases, bringing the total number to 977. Four more deaths were also confirmed, bringing the total to 11.<sup id="cite_ref-292" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-292">[292]</a></sup> Among those infected included a <a href="/wiki/Korean_Air" title="Korean Air">Korean Air</a> crew member.<sup id="cite_ref-293" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-293">[293]</a></sup></li>
<li>Spain, Canary Islands: on the island of Tenerife two Italian hotel guests tested positive for the virus. This resulted in hundreds of guests at the H10 Costa Adeje Palace hotel being isolated to facilitate further testing and to halt the spread of the disease.<sup id="cite_ref-294" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-294">[294]</a></sup>  Later in the day, the first case was reported in mainland Spain, with a woman from Catalonia, who had recently returned from Italy, diagnosed in Barcelona.<sup id="cite_ref-295" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-295">[295]</a></sup> A seventh case was confirmed in the late evening by the  Madrid regional government.<sup id="cite_ref-296" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-296">[296]</a></sup></li>
<li>Switzerland's government announced the first infection in the country.<sup id="cite_ref-Switzerland_297-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Switzerland-297">[297]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Switzerland_de_298-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Switzerland_de-298">[298]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed one more case, an 11-year-old boy, bringing the total number to 31.<sup id="cite_ref-299" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-299">[299]</a></sup></li>
<li>Thailand reported two more cases, taking its total to 37. The two new cases, both Thai nationals, were people who were being monitored due to the travel history of others who had travelled to countries with infection  risks.<sup id="cite_ref-300" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-300">[300]</a></sup></li>
<li>The fourth death associated with <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a> was confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-301" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-301">[301]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="26_February">26 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: 26 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 37:<sup id="cite_ref-302" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-302">[302]</a></sup>
The WHO Director-General, <a href="/wiki/Tedros_Adhanom" title="Tedros Adhanom">Tedros Adhanom</a>, noted that 
"...14 countries that have had cases have not reported a case for more than a week, and even more importantly, 9 countries have not reported a case for more than two weeks: Belgium, Cambodia, Finland, India, Nepal, Philippines, the Russian Federation, Sri Lanka and Sweden."<sup id="cite_ref-303" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-303">[303]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Australia confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 23.<sup id="cite_ref-304" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-304">[304]</a></sup></li>
<li>Bahrain confirmed three additional cases, bringing its total to 26.<sup id="cite_ref-305" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-305">[305]</a></sup> Later in the evening it confirmed another 7 cases, taking the total to 33.<sup id="cite_ref-306" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-306">[306]</a></sup></li>
<li>Canada confirmed a new case in Toronto of a woman with travel history to Iran. This took the country's total to 12.<sup id="cite_ref-307" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-307">[307]</a></sup></li>
<li>Croatia confirmed its second and third cases, the second being the twin brother of the first patient<sup id="cite_ref-308" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-308">[308]</a></sup> and the third being a man who works in Parma, Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-309" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-309">[309]</a></sup></li>
<li>Finland reported its second case.<sup id="cite_ref-310" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-310">[310]</a></sup></li>
<li>France confirmed three new cases, taking it to 17 cases. It also announced its second death from the disease, a 60-year-old French man who had been diagnosed the night before.<sup id="cite_ref-311" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-311">[311]</a></sup> An eighteenth case was later declared.<sup id="cite_ref-312" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-312">[312]</a></sup></li>
<li>Georgia reported its first case in the country, a Georgian native travelling from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-313" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-313">[313]</a></sup></li>
<li>Germany reported five additional cases.<sup id="cite_ref-314" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-314">[314]</a></sup> By the end of the day the overall total number of cases in the country had risen to 27.<sup id="cite_ref-315" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-315">[315]</a></sup></li>
<li>Greece confirmed its first case, a 38-year-old woman who had recently travelled to Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-316" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-316">[316]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong reported six new cases, including a 16-year-old boy and his 21-year-old sister who were both aboard <i>Diamond Princess</i>, bringing the total to 91 cases.<sup id="cite_ref-317" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-317">[317]</a></sup></li>
<li>Italy confirmed 51 additional cases, bringing its total to 374. It also confirmed the twelfth death from the virus.<sup id="cite_ref-318" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-318">[318]</a></sup> In the evening they declared 27 new cases<sup id="cite_ref-319" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-319">[319]</a></sup> followed by an additional 54 cases, with two earlier cases declared false positives.<sup id="cite_ref-320" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-320">[320]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iran confirmed four more deaths, taking the total to 19. Another 44 cases were confirmed, bringing the total number to 139.<sup id="cite_ref-321" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-321">[321]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan confirmed its second death from the virus.<sup id="cite_ref-Japan2Deaths_322-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Japan2Deaths-322">[322]</a></sup> It also reported 5 new confirmed cases in Nagoya. A third death was later confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-323" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-323">[323]</a></sup></li>
<li>Kuwait confirmed that their total of confirmed cases had risen to 12 with one new case. Later that day they confirmed the overall total had risen to 25.<sup id="cite_ref-324" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-324">[324]</a></sup></li>
<li>Lebanon confirmed its second case.<sup id="cite_ref-325" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-325">[325]</a></sup></li>
<li>North Macedonia confirmed its first case, a woman who had recently returned home from Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-326" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-326">[326]</a></sup></li>
<li>Norway confirmed its first case, a person who had returned from China.<sup id="cite_ref-327" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-327">[327]</a></sup></li>
<li>Pakistan confirmed its first case, a 22-year-old man from Sindh province who had travelled to Iran, and also confirmed a second case with no further details.<sup id="cite_ref-328" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-328">[328]</a></sup></li>
<li>Romania confirmed its first case.<sup id="cite_ref-329" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-329">[329]</a></sup></li>
<li>Russia confirmed three more cases, who were passengers on the cruise ship <i>Diamond Princess</i>, bringing the total number to 5.<sup id="cite_ref-330" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-330">[330]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 93.<sup id="cite_ref-331" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-331">[331]</a></sup></li>
<li>Spain confirmed five more cases including a man who was hospitalised in Seville after testing positive, bringing the total number to 12. This was the first confirmed case in the southern region of Andalusia.<sup id="cite_ref-El_Pais_332-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-El_Pais-332">[332]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-333" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-333">[333]</a></sup> Another case was later confirmed in the Canary Islands.<sup id="cite_ref-334" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-334">[334]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed 169 more cases, bringing the total number to 1,146.<sup id="cite_ref-335" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-335">[335]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-336" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-336">[336]</a></sup>  It also recorded an additional death, increasing its total to 12.  In the afternoon, the country reported 115 more infections, bringing the total number to 1,261.<sup id="cite_ref-337" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-337">[337]</a></sup></li>
<li>Sweden reported a new case, the second in the country.<sup id="cite_ref-338" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-338">[338]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed an additional case, bringing its total to 32.<sup id="cite_ref-339" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-339">[339]</a></sup></li>
<li>Thailand confirmed three additional cases, bringing its total to 40 cases.<sup id="cite_ref-340" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-340">[340]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United States confirmed three new cases - one being a domestic case in California with no travel history, and the other two being former passengers aboard <i>Diamond Princess</i> - bringing the total number to 60.<sup id="cite_ref-341" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-341">[341]</a></sup></li>
