<li><i>Diamond Princess</i> saw 14 new confirmed cases, taking it to 705 cases aboard the ship. It is estimated that more passengers on the ship could be infected than previously thought.<sup id="cite_ref-342" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-342">[342]</a></sup></li>
<li>For the first time, a case was re-imported back to China from another country; the patient travelled from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-343" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-343">[343]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="27_February">27 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: 27 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 38:<sup id="cite_ref-344" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-344">[344]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Austria reported its third case, the first in Vienna.<sup id="cite_ref-345" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-345">[345]</a></sup></li>
<li>Canada confirmed the first human-to-human transmission in Toronto, the husband of the woman who had travelled to Iran, bringing the total cases in the country to 13.<sup id="cite_ref-346" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-346">[346]</a></sup> The country later reported a presumptive case in Quebec. The patient had travel history to Iran. This presumptive case was the first case in Quebec, bringing the total number to 14.<sup id="cite_ref-347" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-347">[347]</a></sup></li>
<li>China reported through the National Health Commission 433 new cases and 29 new deaths across the mainland. Of those, 409 cases and 26 deaths were in Hubei province.<sup id="cite_ref-348" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-348">[348]</a></sup></li>
<li>Denmark confirmed its first case, a person who had recently returned from Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-349" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-349">[349]</a></sup></li>
<li>Estonia reported its first case, an Iranian man who had recently returned from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-350" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-350">[350]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-351" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-351">[351]</a></sup></li>
<li>France reported 20 new cases, raising the number of cases in the country to 38.<sup id="cite_ref-352" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-352">[352]</a></sup></li>
<li>Germany saw another case reported in North Rhine-Westphalia.<sup id="cite_ref-353" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-353">[353]</a></sup> In the evening it was reported that there were 14 new cases in the same state, bringing Germany's total to 40 cases.<sup id="cite_ref-354" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-354">[354]</a></sup>  The cases rose to 45 by the end of the day.</li>
<li>Greece confirmed two more cases, the first patient's daughter and another woman in Athens, bringing the total to 3 cases.<sup id="cite_ref-:4_355-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-355">[355]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong reported two additional cases, both women infected after visiting a Hong Kong temple at the centre of a COVID-19 cluster. This took the total number of cases to 93.<sup id="cite_ref-356" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-356">[356]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iran reported that 22 people had now died amid 141 people infected by the virus.<sup id="cite_ref-357" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-357">[357]</a></sup> The chairman of Iran's National Security Committee, <a href="/wiki/Mojtaba_Zolnour" class="mw-redirect" title="Mojtaba Zolnour">Mojtaba Zolnour</a>, announced he had been infected.<sup id="cite_ref-358" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-358">[358]</a></sup>  Iran later announced an increase to 26 deaths and 245 cases.<sup id="cite_ref-359" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-359">[359]</a></sup> The country's Vice President for Women and Family Affairs <a href="/wiki/Masoumeh_Ebtekar" title="Masoumeh Ebtekar">Masoumeh Ebtekar</a> also tested positive.<sup id="cite_ref-360" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-360">[360]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iraq reported a new case associated with travelling to Iran, the sixth in the country and the first in Baghdad.<sup id="cite_ref-361" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-361">[361]</a></sup> A seventh case was confirmed in Kirkuk later in the day.<sup id="cite_ref-362" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-362">[362]</a></sup></li>
<li>Israel reported an additional case, a person who had travelled to Italy, bringing the total number to 3.<sup id="cite_ref-363" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-363">[363]</a></sup></li>
<li>Italy reported that two more people had died, bringing the death toll to 14. The Civil Protection agency reported the number of confirmed cases had risen from 420 to 528.<sup id="cite_ref-364" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-364">[364]</a></sup> Later in the day it was announced that three more people had died, taking the death toll to 17, and the total confirmed cases had risen to 650.<sup id="cite_ref-365" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-365">[365]</a></sup> At the end of the day, the total cases rose to 655.<sup id="cite_ref-366" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-366">[366]</a></sup> Mayor Pietro Mazzocchi of <a href="/wiki/Borgonovo_Val_Tidone" title="Borgonovo Val Tidone">Borgonovo Val Tidone</a> was diagnosed with the virus.<sup id="cite_ref-367" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-367">[367]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan reported 17 new cases. It confirmed a case involving a recovered patient being <a href="/wiki/Coronavirus_disease_2019#Reinfection" title="Coronavirus disease 2019">reinfected</a> with COVID-19. The total number of local cases had increased to 186.<sup id="cite_ref-368" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-368">[368]</a></sup> An eighth person died, a Japanese man in his 80s, who lived in the northern-most island of Hokkaido.<sup id="cite_ref-369" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-369">[369]</a></sup> Additionally, Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Shinzo_Abe" title="Shinzo Abe">Shinzo Abe</a> asked that all elementary, middle, and high schools shall be closed until late March.<sup id="cite_ref-Japan_to_Close_Schools_Nationwide_370-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Japan_to_Close_Schools_Nationwide-370">[370]</a></sup></li>
<li>Kuwait confirmed the total cases in the country were 43, with all having recently travelled to Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-371" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-371">[371]</a></sup></li>
<li>Lebanon reported a third case with the person having travelled from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-372" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-372">[372]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia confirmed an additional case, a woman who had recently travelled to Japan, bringing the total to 23. That made it the first case to be imported from Japan.<sup id="cite_ref-373" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-373">[373]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-374" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-374">[374]</a></sup></li>
<li>The Netherlands reported its first case, a person who had been skiing in Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-375" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-375">[375]</a></sup></li>
<li>Nigeria confirmed its first case, an Italian citizen who worked in Nigeria and returned from Milan. It was the first case of coronavirus in sub-Saharan Africa.<sup id="cite_ref-376" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-376">[376]</a></sup></li>
<li>Norway confirmed three additional cases, two in Oslo and one in Bærum, taking the total to four cases.<sup id="cite_ref-377" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-377">[377]</a></sup> Two returned from Italy and one from Iran.</li>
<li>Oman reported an additional case, raising the country's total to 5.<sup id="cite_ref-378" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-378">[378]</a></sup> An additional case was confirmed later that day, who had travelled from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-379" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-379">[379]</a></sup></li>
<li>San Marino confirmed its first case.<sup id="cite_ref-380" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-380">[380]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number to 96.<sup id="cite_ref-381" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-381">[381]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea reported 334 new cases, bringing the total number to 1,595.<sup id="cite_ref-382" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-382">[382]</a></sup>  171 additional cases were later confirmed, taking the total number to 1,766.<sup id="cite_ref-383" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-383">[383]</a></sup></li>
<li>Spain saw a new case reported in Valencia<sup id="cite_ref-384" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-384">[384]</a></sup> and two more in Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-385" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-385">[385]</a></sup> A further case was reported in Barcelona.<sup id="cite_ref-386" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-386">[386]</a></sup> By the early evening, the total number of confirmed cases had risen to 22.<sup id="cite_ref-387" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-387">[387]</a></sup> In the evening six additional cases were declared in Valencia.<sup id="cite_ref-388" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-388">[388]</a></sup></li>
<li>Sweden had five new cases confirmed, one in the Uppsala region,<sup id="cite_ref-389" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-389">[389]</a></sup> three people in Västra Götaland, and one in the Stockholm region.<sup id="cite_ref-390" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-390">[390]</a></sup></li>
<li>Switzerland reported more cases, with a total of six confirmed cases across five cantons.<sup id="cite_ref-391" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-391">[391]</a></sup>  By the end of the day, a total of eight cases had been detected.</li>
<li>The United Arab Emirates reported the recovery of two patients, and six new cases, bringing the total number to 19.<sup id="cite_ref-392" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-392">[392]</a></sup> It also saw two suspected cases attached to the UAE Tour, a cycling event, which resulted in the cancellation of the event.<sup id="cite_ref-393" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-393">[393]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United Kingdom confirmed two more cases, contracted in Italy and Tenerife, taking the total to 15 cases.<sup id="cite_ref-394" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-394">[394]</a></sup> In the evening, a sixteenth case was confirmed, and the first case in Northern Ireland, someone who had come from Italy via Dublin.<sup id="cite_ref-395" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-395">[395]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="28_February">28 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: 28 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Communiqu%C3%A9_de_presse_du_Conseil_f%C3%A9d%C3%A9ral,_28.02.2020_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Communiqu%C3%A9_de_presse_du_Conseil_f%C3%A9d%C3%A9ral%2C_28.02.2020_%28cropped%29.jpg/220px-Communiqu%C3%A9_de_presse_du_Conseil_f%C3%A9d%C3%A9ral%2C_28.02.2020_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Communiqu%C3%A9_de_presse_du_Conseil_f%C3%A9d%C3%A9ral%2C_28.02.2020_%28cropped%29.jpg/330px-Communiqu%C3%A9_de_presse_du_Conseil_f%C3%A9d%C3%A9ral%2C_28.02.2020_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Communiqu%C3%A9_de_presse_du_Conseil_f%C3%A9d%C3%A9ral%2C_28.02.2020_%28cropped%29.jpg/440px-Communiqu%C3%A9_de_presse_du_Conseil_f%C3%A9d%C3%A9ral%2C_28.02.2020_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="615" data-file-height="870" width="220" height="311"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Communiqu%C3%A9_de_presse_du_Conseil_f%C3%A9d%C3%A9ral,_28.02.2020_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Press release of the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Council_(Switzerland)" title="Federal Council (Switzerland)">Swiss government</a> banning events of more than 1,000 people (28 February 2020).</div></div></div>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 39:<sup id="cite_ref-396" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-396">[396]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Australia confirmed one additional case, a former <i>Diamond Princess</i> passenger now in Western Australia, bringing the total number to 24.<sup id="cite_ref-397" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-397">[397]</a></sup></li>
<li>Azerbaijan confirmed its first case, a Russian national who recently returned from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-398" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-398">[398]</a></sup></li>
<li>Bahrain announced three new cases, raising the total to 36.<sup id="cite_ref-399" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-399">[399]</a></sup> An additional two cases were later confirmed, both having recently travelled from Iran, one being a Saudi Arabian national.<sup id="cite_ref-400" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-400">[400]</a></sup></li>
<li>Belarus confirmed its first case, a student from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-401" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-401">[401]</a></sup></li>
<li>Canada reported two positive cases in Ontario. One of them had travel history to Iran, while the other had visited Egypt.<sup id="cite_ref-402" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-402">[402]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-403" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-403">[403]</a></sup> The total number of cases rose to 16.</li>
<li>China confirmed an additional 327 new confirmed cases, of which 318 were in the province of Hubei. There were 44 deaths of which 41 were in Hubei, one in Xinjiang and two in Beijing.<sup id="cite_ref-404" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-404">[404]</a></sup></li>
<li>Croatia confirmed two new cases, one being the girlfriend of the first patient and the other the wife of the third patient, bringing the total number to 5.<sup id="cite_ref-405" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-405">[405]</a></sup></li>
<li>Denmark confirmed an additional case, bringing the total number to 2.<sup id="cite_ref-406" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-406">[406]</a></sup></li>
<li>Finland confirmed an additional case, taking it to 3 confirmed cases.<sup id="cite_ref-407" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-407">[407]</a></sup></li>
<li>France announced two new cases, bringing the total number to 40.<sup id="cite_ref-408" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-408">[408]</a></sup>  The total number of cases later rose to 57.</li>
<li>Georgia confirmed a second case, a citizen who had returned from Italy. More than 18 people were reported to be in quarantine.<sup id="cite_ref-409" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-409">[409]</a></sup></li>
<li>Germany reported cases totalling "almost 60", according to a Health Ministry official.<sup id="cite_ref-410" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-410">[410]</a></sup></li>
<li>Greece confirmed an additional case, who had recently travelled to Italy. This was the country's fourth case.<sup id="cite_ref-411" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-411">[411]</a></sup></li>
<li>Hong Kong confirmed an additional case, a patient from <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Princess_(ship)" title="Diamond Princess (ship)"><i>Diamond Princess</i></a>, bringing the total number to 94.<sup id="cite_ref-412" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-412">[412]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iceland confirmed its first case, a person who had returned from Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-413" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-413">[413]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iran confirmed 143 new cases and 6 more deaths, with a total of 388 cases and 32 deaths.<sup id="cite_ref-414" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-414">[414]</a></sup> Four MP's had tested positive, an increase from the two who had already announced their cases.<sup id="cite_ref-415" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-415">[415]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iraq confirmed an eighth case, a woman who recently came back from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-416" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-416">[416]</a></sup></li>
<li>Israel confirmed an additional case, the second in the country - the wife of the previous person diagnosed.<sup id="cite_ref-417" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-417">[417]</a></sup> Five additional cases were later confirmed, taking the total to 7. One of the new cases was an Israeli who had recovered in Japan, who was diagnosed again after returning.<sup id="cite_ref-418" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-418">[418]</a></sup></li>
<li>Italy reported that four more people had died, bringing the death toll to 21. The number of confirmed cases had risen from 650 (the day before) to 888.<sup id="cite_ref-419" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-419">[419]</a></sup></li>
<li>Japan announced an additional death, bringing the total to 5.<sup id="cite_ref-420" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-420">[420]</a></sup>  They also confirmed 12 new cases in Hokkaido. Japan also later confirmed another death regarding a British native on board <i>Diamond Princess</i>, marking the first foreign victim on the cruise ship.<sup id="cite_ref-421" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-421">[421]</a></sup></li>
<li>Kuwait announced two additional cases, taking its total to 45.<sup id="cite_ref-422" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-422">[422]</a></sup></li>
<li>Lebanon confirmed its fourth case, a Syrian man, the first case of local transmission.<sup id="cite_ref-423" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-423">[423]</a></sup></li>
<li>Lithuania confirmed its first case, a woman who returned from Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-424" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-424">[424]</a></sup></li>
<li>Malaysia confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 25.<sup id="cite_ref-CNAMY28Feb_425-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNAMY28Feb-425">[425]</a></sup></li>
<li>Mexico confirmed its first two cases, one in Mexico City and one in Culiacán.<sup id="cite_ref-426" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-426">[426]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-427" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-427">[427]</a></sup> Both cases were individuals who recently returned from a trip to Bergamo, Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-428" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-428">[428]</a></sup></li>
<li>Monaco saw the government confirm the first case in the principality.<sup id="cite_ref-429" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-429">[429]</a></sup></li>
<li>New Zealand confirmed its first case, an individual who had returned from Iran to Auckland earlier in the week.<sup id="cite_ref-Stuff_28_Feb_2020_430-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stuff_28_Feb_2020-430">[430]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Radio_NZ_28_Feb_2020_431-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Radio_NZ_28_Feb_2020-431">[431]</a></sup></li>
<li>The Netherlands confirmed its second case.<sup id="cite_ref-432" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-432">[432]</a></sup></li>
<li>Norway confirmed two other cases, with the second having serious implications. First it was confirmed that a person from Bergen, who returned from Italy, tested positive. Later it was confirmed that a person working at Ullevaal Hospital in Oslo also tested positive, after having returned from Italy. According to standard recommendation he was told to go to work, since he had no symptoms, and he had worked with a significant number of patients for a couple of days before testing positive. Norway now has 6 confirmed cases.<sup id="cite_ref-433" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-433">[433]</a></sup></li>
<li>Romania confirmed two new cases, both having recently returned from Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-434" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-434">[434]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed two more cases, bringing the total number to 98.<sup id="cite_ref-435" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-435">[435]</a></sup></li>
<li>Spain confirmed more cases, taking it to 32 cases with 5 in Madrid, 8 in Comunidad Valenciana, 6 in the Canary Islands, 6 in Catalonia, 1 in the Balearic Islands, 6 in Andalucía, 1 in Aragón and 2 in Castilla y León.<sup id="cite_ref-436" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-436">[436]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed 256 new cases, bringing the total number of infected in the country to 2,022. 182 of the new cases were in Daegu.<sup id="cite_ref-437" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-437">[437]</a></sup> There were three new deaths, raising the number to 16.<sup id="cite_ref-438" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-438">[438]</a></sup> Later, the number of cases there shot up by 315, bringing the total number to 2,337.<sup id="cite_ref-439" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-439">[439]</a></sup></li>
<li>Sweden confirmed four more cases, raising the country's total to 11.<sup id="cite_ref-440" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-440">[440]</a></sup></li>
<li>Switzerland's cases increased to 15.<sup id="cite_ref-441" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-441">[441]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed two additional cases, taking its total to 34.<sup id="cite_ref-442" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-442">[442]</a></sup></li>
<li>Thailand confirmed an additional case, taking the overall number to 41.<sup id="cite_ref-443" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-443">[443]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United Kingdom reported its 17th and 18th cases, in people who had travelled from Iran, and its 19th case and the first in Wales, being someone who had travelled from Northern Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-444" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-444">[444]</a></sup> In the evening, the 20th case was confirmed, the first case of being passed on in the UK from an unknown source.<sup id="cite_ref-445" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-445">[445]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United States confirmed 4 more cases, including 2 former passengers of <i>Diamond Princess</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-446" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-446">[446]</a></sup> Washington state authorities later confirmed two additional presumptive cases, bringing its total to 66. One had recently returned from South Korea, and the other case was unrelated and locally acquired.<sup id="cite_ref-447" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-447">[447]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-448" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-448">[448]</a></sup></li>
<li>SARS-CoV-2 was detected for the first time in tears and conjunctival secretions (pink eye) of a patient. This was only detected in 1 out of the 30 patients that were tested. The excerpt from the study stated, "In the study of this small sample, we used conjunctival test paper to obtain tears and conjunctival secretions of 30 patients for standard RT-PCR assay. Only one patient with conjunctivitis found viral RNA in his tear fluid and conjunctival secretion twice."<sup id="cite_ref-449" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-449">[449]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="29_February">29 February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_in_February_2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: 29 February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>WHO</b> Situation Report 40:<sup id="cite_ref-450" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-450">[450]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Australia confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 25.<sup id="cite_ref-Aus29Feb_451-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Aus29Feb-451">[451]</a></sup></li>
<li>Austria confirmed four new cases, bringing the total to 10.<sup id="cite_ref-452" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-452">[452]</a></sup></li>
<li>Azerbaijan reported two new cases, both recently returned from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-453" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-453">[453]</a></sup></li>
<li>Bahrain confirmed three additional cases, all who had travelled to Iran, bringing the total number to 41.<sup id="cite_ref-454" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-454">[454]</a></sup></li>
<li>Brazil confirmed the second case, a 32-year-old man who arrived from Milan, Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-455" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-455">[455]</a></sup></li>
<li>Canada confirmed four new cases, three in Ontario and one in <a href="/wiki/British_Columbia" title="British Columbia">British Columbia</a>, bringing the total to 20.<sup id="cite_ref-456" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-456">[456]</a></sup></li>
<li>China confirmed 427 new cases - 423 of which were in Hubei province - bringing the total number to 79,251. Deaths increased by 47, to a total of 2,835.<sup id="cite_ref-457" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-457">[457]</a></sup></li>
<li>Croatia confirmed its sixth case, a close relative of the third and fifth patients.<sup id="cite_ref-458" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-458">[458]</a></sup></li>
<li>Denmark confirmed its third case, a person recently returned from a trip to Munich, Germany, where he came into contact with someone who was later determined to have the virus.<sup id="cite_ref-459" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-459">[459]</a></sup></li>
<li>Ecuador confirmed its first case, a woman who recently returned from a trip to Spain.<sup id="cite_ref-460" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-460">[460]</a></sup></li>
<li>France confirmed 16 additional cases, bringing the total number to 73.<sup id="cite_ref-CNAFrance29Feb_461-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNAFrance29Feb-461">[461]</a></sup> Additional cases were confirmed, taking the number to 100.<sup id="cite_ref-462" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-462">[462]</a></sup></li>
<li>Georgia confirmed one new case, taking the total number to 3.<sup id="cite_ref-463" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-463">[463]</a></sup></li>
<li>Germany's confirmed cases increased to 66.<sup id="cite_ref-464" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-464">[464]</a></sup></li>
<li>Greece confirmed three new cases, two of which were close contacts of a previous confirmed case, the other had travelled to Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-465" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-465">[465]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iran confirmed 205 new cases, and 9 new deaths, bringing the total to 593 infected and 43 dead.<sup id="cite_ref-466" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-466">[466]</a></sup></li>
<li>Iraq confirmed 5 new cases, bringing the total number to 13. Four of them are in Baghdad and the fifth is in Babil province.<sup id="cite_ref-467" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-467">[467]</a></sup></li>
<li>Ireland confirmed its first case, associated with travel to northern Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-468" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-468">[468]</a></sup></li>
<li>Italy confirmed 239 new cases and 8 new deaths, bringing it to 1,128 cases and 29 deaths.<sup id="cite_ref-469" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-469">[469]</a></sup></li>
<li>Lebanon confirmed three more cases, bringing the total number of cases to seven.<sup id="cite_ref-470" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-470">[470]</a></sup></li>
<li>Luxembourg confirmed its first case.<sup id="cite_ref-471" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-471">[471]</a></sup></li>
<li>Mexico confirmed two more cases, one man in the State of Mexico who participated in the same trip to Bergamo, Italy, that the first two infected made,<sup id="cite_ref-472" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-472">[472]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-473" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-473">[473]</a></sup> and a woman in Coahuila who traveled to Milan, Italy, between January and February,<sup id="cite_ref-474" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-474">[474]</a></sup> bringing the total to 4.</li>
<li>The Netherlands confirmed four additional cases, bringing the total to 6.<sup id="cite_ref-475" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-475">[475]</a></sup> A seventh case was later confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-476" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-476">[476]</a></sup></li>
<li>Norway confirmed nine new cases, bringing the total to 15.<sup id="cite_ref-477" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-477">[477]</a></sup></li>
<li>Pakistan confirmed two mores cases, bringing its total to 4. One is a person from Karachi who had recently traveled to Iran, and the other case was in the Federal Area.<sup id="cite_ref-478" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-478">[478]</a></sup></li>
<li>Qatar confirmed its first case, a Qatari national who had recently returned from Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-479" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-479">[479]</a></sup></li>
<li>Singapore confirmed four more cases, bringing the total number to 102.<sup id="cite_ref-480" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-480">[480]</a></sup></li>
<li>South Korea confirmed 594 more cases, bringing the total number to 2,931.<sup id="cite_ref-481" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-481">[481]</a></sup> This later increased with another 219 cases declared, bringing the total number to 3,150. Another death was confirmed, bringing the total to 17.<sup id="cite_ref-482" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-482">[482]</a></sup> The first reinfection case was also confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-483" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-483">[483]</a></sup></li>
<li>Spain confirmed 26 more cases, bringing the total number to 58.<sup id="cite_ref-484" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-484">[484]</a></sup></li>
<li>Sweden reported two new cases, taking the total to 13.<sup id="cite_ref-485" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-485">[485]</a></sup></li>
<li>Switzerland confirmed 3 more cases, bringing the total number to 18.<sup id="cite_ref-486" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-486">[486]</a></sup></li>
<li>Taiwan confirmed five more cases, bringing the total number to 39.<sup id="cite_ref-487" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-487">[487]</a></sup></li>
<li>Thailand confirmed one more case, bringing the total number to 42.<sup id="cite_ref-488" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-488">[488]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United Kingdom confirmed three additional cases, taking the total to 23.<sup id="cite_ref-489" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-489">[489]</a></sup></li>
<li>The United States confirmed its first death, a man from <a href="/wiki/Washington_(state)" title="Washington (state)">Washington</a> near the <a href="/wiki/Seattle" title="Seattle">Seattle</a> area.<sup id="cite_ref-490" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-490">[490]</a></sup> The country also reported two more cases, bringing the total number to 68.<sup id="cite_ref-491" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-491">[491]</a></sup></li></ul>
